But the overrides still get processed. If those field overrides depend on the defaults having cellOptions already set up, there's a structural mismatch. And given the task description mentions \"Dashboards without explicit `fieldConfig.defaults.custom` lose column widths and text alignment,\" it's clear the overrides contain this styling data but can't be properly applied without the defaults structure being initialized first.\n\nLooking at the Go code more carefully, there's a critical condition: if `fieldConfig[\"defaults\"]` doesn't exist at all, the entire block gets skipped before `migrateOverrides` even runs. Migration Implementation Files\\n- **Primary File**: `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/v38.go` - Contains the V38 migration function and all fieldConfig handling logic\\n- **Registration File**: `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/migrations.go` (line 74) - Registers V38 in the migration pipeline  \\n- **Defaults Management**: `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/frontend_defaults.go` - Handles application of frontend defaults and preservation of field config structures\\n\\n#### 2. The Flawed Conditional Logic (v38.go, lines 116-127)\\nThe problematic nested condition is:\\n```go\\nif defaults, ok := fieldConfig[\\\"defaults\\\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\\n    if custom, ok := defaults[\\\"custom\\\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\\n        // Migrate displayMode to cellOptions in defaults\\n        if displayMode, exists := custom[\\\"displayMode\\\"]; exists {\\n            if displayModeStr, ok := displayMode.(string); ok {\\n                custom[\\\"cellOptions\\\"] = migrateTableDisplayModeToCellOptions(displayModeStr)\\n            }\\n            delete(custom, \\\"displayMode\\\")\\n        }\\n    }\\n}\\n```\\n\\n**The Bug**: When `defaults` exists but `defaults.custom` does NOT exist, the inner condition (line 117) fails, and the entire block (lines 116-127) is exited. This causes silent loss of configuration data when:\\n- A table panel has `fieldConfig.defaults` but no `fieldConfig.defaults.custom` object\\n- That panel has field overrides specifying `custom.displayMode` for column widths and text alignment  \\n- The migration fails to ensure `custom` object existence before processing overrides that reference `custom.*` properties\\n\\n#### 3. The Override Migration Function (lines 135-176)\\nThe `migrateOverrides` function correctly processes field override rules that reference `custom.displayMode` and converts them to `custom.cellOptions`. However, it operates independently and cannot address the missing base `custom` structure in defaults.\\n\\n#### 4. Related Context: Unsafe Code Pattern in v35.go (lines 67-70)\\nA similar but more severe issue exists in the v35 migration:\\n```go\\ndefaults, _ := fieldConfig[\\\"defaults\\\"].(map[string]interface{})\\ncustom, _ := defaults[\\\"custom\\\"].(map[string]interface{})\\nif custom[\\\"axisPlacement\\\"] != \\\"hidden\\\" {\\n    return\\n}\\n```\\nThis code silently ignores type assertion errors using underscore (`_`), which causes nil pointer dereferences when `defaults` or `custom` don't exist.\\n\\n#### 5. The Root Cause Pattern\\nDashboards that import with `fieldConfig` containing only `overrides` (no `defaults.custom`) lose override configuration because:\\n1. `applyPanelDefaults` (frontend_defaults.go) only ensures `defaults` and `overrides` exist, NOT `defaults.custom`\\n2. V38's conditional on line 116-117 requires both `defaults` AND `custom` to exist before processing\\n3. When `custom` doesn't exist, the migration skips the nested block but overrides still need the base `custom` structure to be valid\\n4. Field overrides referencing `custom.*` properties become orphaned without the parent `custom` object in defaults\\n\\n#### 6. The Register Point\\nThe V38 migration is registered in `GetMigrations()` at line 74 of `migrations.go`:\\n```go\\n38: V38,\\n```\\nThis ensures V38 runs in the schema version migration pipeline between v37 and v39.\\n\\n### Impact\\nDashboards without explicit `fieldConfig.defaults.custom` lose column widths and text alignment settings that were stored as field overrides, breaking visual layout on import.\\n\"","stderr":"","interrupted":false,"isImage":false,"noOutputExpected":false}}
